      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 1st century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 100 to 1 BC there were 251
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 92 were partial, 77 were annular, 65 were total (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), and 17 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 17 different years: 99 BC, 81 BC, 77 BC, 70 BC, 63 BC, 59 BC, 52 BC, 48 BC, 45 BC, 41 BC, 34 BC, 30 BC, 27 BC, 23 BC, 16 BC, 12 BC, and 5 BC.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

            <th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:1%">
             Visibility
            </th>
            <td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
             <div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
